<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/orenge#Middle_English" title="orenge">orenge</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/orange#Middle_English" title="orange">orange</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pome_orenge&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pome orenge (page does not exist)">pome orenge</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">fruit orange</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro"><a href="/wiki/auranja#Old_Occitan" title="auranja">auranja</a></i> and calqued from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/melarancio#Italian" title="melarancio">melarancio</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/melarancia#Italian" title="melarancia">melarancia</a></i>, compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/mela#Italian" title="mela">mela</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/arancia#Italian" title="arancia">(n)arancia</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">orange</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%86%D8%A7%D8%B1%D9%86%D8%AC#Arabic" title="ŸÜÿßÿ±ŸÜÿ¨">ŸÜŸéÿßÿ±ŸéŸÜŸíÿ¨</a></i>‚Äé <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nƒÅranj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa"><a href="/wiki/%D9%86%D8%A7%D8%B1%D9%86%DA%AF#Persian" title="ŸÜÿßÿ±ŸÜ⁄Ø">ŸÜÿßÿ±ŸÜ⁄Ø</a></i>‚Äé <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">n√¢rang</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/wiki/%E0%A4%A8%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%99%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%97#Sanskrit" title="‡§®‡§æ‡§∞‡§ô‡•ç‡§ó">‡§®‡§æ‡§∞‡§ô‡•ç‡§ó</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nƒÅra·πÖga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">orange tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dravidian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Dravidian languages">Dravidian</a></span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tamil_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tamil href="/w/index.php?title=%E0%AE%A8%E0%AE%BE%E0%AE%B0%E0%AF%8D%E0%AE%A4%E0%AF%8D%E0%AE%A4%E0%AE%99%E0%AF%8D%E0%AE%95%E0%AE%BE%E0%AE%AF%E0%AF%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" </p><p>For other similar cases of the incorrect division (or, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elision" class="extiw" title="w:Elision">elision</a>/<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rebracketing" class="extiw" title="w:Rebracketing">rebracketing</a>) of the above Italian word, but in English, see <a href="/wiki/Category:English_rebracketings" title="Category:English rebracketings">Category:English rebracketings</a>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">orange</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oranges#English" title="oranges">oranges</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href="/wiki/evergreen" title="evergreen">evergreen</a> <a href="/wiki/tree" title="tree">tree</a> of the genus <i><a href="/wiki/Citrus" title="Citrus">Citrus</a></i> such as <i><a href="/wiki/Citrus_sinensis" title="Citrus sinensis">Citrus sinensis</a></i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href="/wiki/fruit" title="fruit">fruit</a> of the orange tree; a <a href="/wiki/citrus_fruit" title="citrus fruit">citrus fruit</a> with a slightly <a href="/wiki/sour" title="sour">sour</a> flavour.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/colour" title="colour">colour</a> of a ripe fruit of an orange tree, midway between red and yellow.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">orange: <span style="background-color:#FFA500; display:inline-block; width:80px;">&nbsp;</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/yellowred#English" title="yellowred">yellowred</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Various drinks:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Orange juice.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An orange-coloured and orange-flavoured <a href="/wiki/cordial" title="cordial">cordial</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An orange-coloured and orange-flavoured <a href="/wiki/soft_drink" title="soft drink">soft drink</a>.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>It is commonly stated that ‚Äúorange‚Äù has no rhymes. While there are no commonly used English dictionary words that rhyme exactly with ‚Äúorange‚Äù (‚Äúdoor-hinge‚Äù comes close in US pronunciation), the English surname <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Gorringe#English" title="Gorringe">Gorringe</a></i> is a rhyme, at least in UK pronunciation. See <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orange_(word)#Rhyme" class="extiw" title="w:Orange (word)">the Wikipedia article about rhymes for the word ‚Äúorange‚Äù</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">orange</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparative" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oranger#English" title="oranger">oranger</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/more#English" title="more">more</a> orange</b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#superlative" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/orangest#English" title="orangest">orangest</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/most#English" title="most">most</a> orange</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having the <a href="/wiki/colour" title="colour">colour</a> of the fruit of an orange tree; <a href="/wiki/yellowred" title="yellowred">yellowred</a>; reddish-yellow.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Antonyms">Antonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Antonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">orange</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oranges#English" title="oranges">oranges</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oranging#English" title="oranging">oranging</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oranged#English" title="oranged">oranged</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To color orange.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  Gilles Deleuze,  <cite>Cinema: The movement-image</cite>, page 118:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It is this composition which reaches a colourist perfection in Le Bonheur with the complementarity of violet, purple and <b>oranged</b> gold</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1987</b>,  Harold Keith,  <cite>Rifles for Watie</cite>, page 256:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Jeff winked his eyes sleepily open and looked out into the cool flush of early morning. The east was <b>oranged</b> over with daybreak.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Suzanne Crowley,  <cite>The Very Ordered Existence of Merilee Marvelous</cite>, page 117:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I looked at him through my binoculars, his little lips <b>oranged</b> with Cheeto dust.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become orange.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Ter√©zia Mora,  <cite>Day in day out</cite>, page 296:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Cranes in the distance against the background of the slowly <b>oranging</b> sky</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  Wanda Coleman, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>, page 14:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It will be followed by a disappearance of the cash I had hidden in a sealed envelope behind the <b>oranging</b> Modigliani print over the living room couch.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Justin Cronin,  <cite>The Passage</cite>, page 330:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"What about his eyes?" / "Nothing. No <b>oranging</b> at all, from what I could see.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="French">French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: French">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Short form of late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pume_orenge&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pume orenge (page does not exist)">pume orenge</a></i> or <i>pomme d'orenge</i>, which was calqued after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/melarancia#Italian" title="melarancia">melarancia</a></i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/mela#Italian" title="mela">mela</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/arancia#Italian" title="arancia">arancia</a></i>). The <i>o</i> came into the word under influence of the place name <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/Orange#French" title="Orange">Orange</a></i>, from where these fruits came to the north.
See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/orange#English" title="orange">orange</a></i> (English).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">orange</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/oranges#French" title="oranges">oranges</a></b>)

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Il pressa l‚Äô<b>orange</b> afin d‚Äôen extraire du jus.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He squeezed the <b>orange</b> to extract juice from it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Derived terms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">orange</strong> (<i>invariable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/orange#English" title="orange">orange</a></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Les premiers TGV atlantiques √©taient <b>orange</b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The first Atlantic TGV trains were <b>orange</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd>While theoretically the adjective <i>orange</i> is invariable, being (originally) a colour name derived from a noun, the nonstandard plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/oranges#French" title="oranges">oranges</a></i> is in use.</dd></dl>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="German">German</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: German">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Orange#German" title="Orange">Orange</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">orange fruit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/orange#French" title="orange">orange</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">predicative only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:German_pronunciation" title="Appendix:German pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å√£Àê É/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Åa≈ã É/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å…îÃÉÀê É/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å…î≈ã É/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">non-predicative feminine and plural forms</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:German_pronunciation" title="Appendix:German pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å√£Àê í…ô/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Åa≈ã í…ô/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å…îÃÉÀê í…ô/</span>, <span class="IPA">/oÀà Å…î≈ã í…ô/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio</td><td class="audiofile"><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:175px"><div class="mwPlayerContainer k-player" style="width: 175px; position: relative; height: 20px;"><div class="videoHolder"><div class="mwEmbedPlayer" id="mwe_player_3" style=""><img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mNkqAcAAIUAgUW0RjgAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" class="playerPoster" style="position: absolute; inset: 0px 0px 0px 77.5px; height: 20px; width: 20px;"></div><div title="Play clip" class="play-btn-large" style="left: 50%; top: 50%; margin-left: -35px; margin-top: -27.5px;"></div></div><div class="ui-state-default ui-widget-header ui-helper-clearfix control-bar block" style="height: 20px;"><div title="Player options" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-bl rButton k-options"><span>Menu</span></div><div class="ui-slider ui-slider-horizontal rButton volume-slider ui-widget ui-widget-content ui-corner-all"><div class="ui-slider-range ui-widget-header ui-slider-range-min" style="width: 80%;"></div><a class="ui-slider-handle ui-state-default ui-corner-all" href="#" style="left: 80%;"></a></div><div title="Volume control" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-all ui-icon_link rButton volume_control"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-volume-on"></span></div><div class="ui-widget time-disp">0:00</div><div title="Play clip" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-all ui-icon_link lButton play-btn"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-play"></span></div></div></div></div></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:De-orange.ogg" title="File:De-orange.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de">orange</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparative" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/oranger#German" title="oranger">oranger</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/orangener#German" title="orangener">orangener</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#superlative" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am <a href="/wiki/orangesten#German" title="orangesten">orangesten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am <a href="/wiki/orangensten#German" title="orangensten">orangensten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="#English">orange</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>The adjective has two sets of forms. In the formal standard language, endings are added directly to the stem (<i>orang-</i>). In less formal style and in the vernacular, another set of forms is used in free variation, in which an <i>-n-</i> is infixed before the endings.</li>
<li>It is also officially correct to leave the adjective entirely undeclined. This usage is rare, however, and seems dated.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Declension">Declension</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=orange&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Declension">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
